## Section 009: Agent Usage Decision Guide
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 009 "Agent Usage Decision Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed four generic bullets stand where the guide defines a lean agent economy, the authoring agent who follows the six-step process, the skill-reviewer agent invoked by a plain-language request to check best practices, and the future consuming Claude instance the whole artifact is written for, three roles connected by the write-for-the-reader thesis
- **supporting_reason:** Section 009 "Agent Usage Decision Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the roles partition by time, the author works now, the reviewer checks now, and the consumer executes later with no channel back to the author except skill revision, so authoring quality is the only message that reaches the future reader
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 009 "Agent Usage Decision Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: collapsing author and reviewer loses the fresh-eyes check the reviewer exists for, and forgetting the future consumer produces the human-audience prose the mistake catalog documents

## Section 023: Performance Verification Method
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed latency packet stands beside this lineage's actual performance doctrine, skill cost is context cost, measured in words at three loading levels, roughly 100 always-loaded description words, a body budget with 1500-2000 ideal and 5k hard ceiling paid on every trigger, and unlimited reference capacity paid only on demand, with scripts costing nothing to execute unread
- **supporting_reason:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because every triggered skill taxes the context window before any work happens, so the guide prices content by loading level and pushes weight down-level, the whole progressive-disclosure design is a performance optimization stated as document structure
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: unpriced content accumulates at the always-loaded and per-trigger levels, the 8000-word monolith exhibit is a performance bug wearing a documentation costume
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: performance of skills as context investments, runtime performance of skill-invoked scripts belongs to their domains
- **revision_decision:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to state the three-level cost model with its budgets and the down-level migration rule as this theme's verification method
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that the asterisk on unlimited bundled resources is the model's sharpest line, scripts can be executed without being read, making execution the only zero-context-cost consumption mode, which quietly explains the ancestor's script preference for repeated code, moving work from tokens to processes is the lineage's deepest performance move

## Section 024: Scale Boundary Statement
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed task-splitting bounds stand beside the documents' own scale limits, a skill scales until its body hits the disclosure ceiling, then splits into references, references scale until they exceed 10k words, then need grep patterns in the body, and the plugin scales skills by directory, auto-discovery finds any subdirectory with a SKILL.md, making the skills directory the unit that absorbs growth
- **supporting_reason:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because each container has a designed overflow route, body to references, references to searchable references, plugin to more skills, so scaling doctrine here is a chain of graceful spillovers rather than a single ceiling
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: ignoring an overflow route breaks the next level up, an overgrown body defeats triggering economics, an unsearchable 15k-word reference defeats on-demand loading, and one mega-skill defeats the plugin's per-domain triggering
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: bounding skill and plugin growth, the corpus's own document scale limits belong to its process themes
- **revision_decision:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to name the three-level spillover chain with its thresholds, the word ladder, the 10k grep rule, and directory-per-domain splitting
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that the 10k grep-pattern rule is progressive disclosure applied recursively, when a reference outgrows loading whole, the skill discloses search patterns instead of content, pointing the reader at retrieval rather than text, the same move the corpus makes with its own oversized sources, spilled scale becomes an indexing problem at every level
